Mchyen-brtse (Mtshan-tho)

KARCHAK
Mari med bshes gnyen dang ni sangs rgyas gseng/
ff. 90v-93v
/(bsam yas rab gnas mkhan) shāntim garbha rnam dag seng ge dang/
/pagma'i ngang tshul bram ze à nanda/
/kalpa mi tra dzi na mi tra dang/
lha abang byang chub shi lendra bo dhi/
/aa na shi la bo dhi mi tra dang/
mu ni warme sarba dunyä de ba/
/(bidyā ka ra pra bhā) rig byed od zer bya ba la sogs dang/
freya nag slob dpen me hā de ba che/
ma hã ya na bya ba la sogs byon/
/de de'i snyan du skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang/
Mun gyi sngon ma thon mi sambho te/
Maharna koştha (f. lv) dang ni rdo rje dpal/
/(bran ka) mū la ko sa ye shes (gnyags) gzhon nu dang/
Angan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs ba ye shes dbang/
/(sba khri gzher) sam shi ta dang sbrang rgyar legs gzigs mtshan/
/seng gdong lha lung gzigs dang rba gsal snang dang/
/(sna nam) rdo rje baud 'joms (lce) aznyā na siddhi'i mtshan/
/(mchims) shakya pra bhā dza ya (brang ti) rakşi ta/
/(shud bu) dpal gyi seng ge manydzu shri dba'/
/lha abang srung dang bran ka ma ti ke/
/rnam par snang mdzad srung dang klu dbang srungs/
/rin chen mchog dang rin chen legs par grub/
Maharmā lo ka dran pa nam mkha' dang/
/rnam par mi rtog shakya 'od dang rtse/
Achyi 'brug dang ni khams pa nyang go cha dunya/
/de ba ko sa rgyal myen (zhang)nya bzang dang/
l'gos (f. 2r) lo chos 'grub stong gi ā tsar.ya/



harma sht la (cog ro) klu yi rgyal mtshan dang/
apal brtsegs srungs dang ratna raksi ta/
/ye shes sde dang dza ya rakşi ta/
/'jam dpal go cha ratnendra sbI la/
bzang skyong lha yi za ba dpal gyi lhun/
/apal gyi 'byor pa ye shes snying po can/
/rgyal ba shes rab shakya bshes gyen dang/
lage ba dpal dang legs sde nam mkha'i snying/
/yig mkhan dgon gling rma dang gzhon nu srung/
/nam mkha' skyong ste skad gnyis smra mnams kyis/
/dam pa'i chos mang bod kyi skad du begyur/
/bstan pa phyi dar dus kyi pandi ta/
/buddha pa la dharma pā la dang/
/pradznyā pă la dang ni legs par bshad/
/shraddhā ka ra warmma padma sbas/
mukti mi tra sangs reyas dpal zhi ba/
shes rab go cha dpal ldan jo bo a ti sha/
/(de'1 dbon) da na shi la dran pa ye shes grags/
/phra la ring ba su na ya shri dang/
Acha che dznyä na shri dang tsā ndra rā hu la/
/('bum phrag gsum pa) ah ra pa la a tu lya da sha/
blo bzang grags pa a ma ra tsandra/
/thig le bum pa gzhon nu bum pa dang/
Igser gyi go cha dam pa rgya gar ba/
faza ya nanda ga ya dha ra'i zhabs/
/don yod rdo rje kha che zla ba mgon/
/stong nyid ting 'dzin rdo rje ye rdor bal
/shes rab gsang ba ma, hã dza na dang/
/stobs kyi zla ba mantra ka laku/
karma badzra dang ni dza mă ri/
/dpa' bo rdo rje sgra gcan'dzin sbas pa/ (f. 20)
Imam snang rdo rje manydzu cho şa dang/
/su r.ye ki rti pradznyā shri dunya na/
ganggă dhā ra dang ni nor sbas dang/
kun bzang dpal dang nişka langka lha/
/gro bshes aga' dang buddha shrI dznyā na/
/shākya shri rab 'byor zla ba bzang/
/su ga ta shri dã na shi la dang/
Maza ya datta dang ni sa gha shri/
/blo bzang snying po kā la tsandra dang/
lazi na gupta ma hã bo dhi pas/



Mkhyen-brtse (Mtshan-tho)
aza ma bha shri 'jig rten geum kun pa/
Alongs spyod rdo rje dang ni ratna shri/
/(bal po) ma hā se na badzra kirti dang/
/ka ya shri dang bal po grags pa dpal/
Aku mā ra dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal/
/sa dhu kirti bi na ya shri dang/
/shi la shri dang ganggā (sic!) la shrI dang/
/bi ma la shri darpa pa ā tsar.ya/
/rgyal ba'i lhe dang lakşmi ka ra/
là nanda shri rā hu la shri dang/
Izang gling pa dang kirti pandi ta/
/sha ri sū tra nags kyi rin chen dang/
/buddha gupta zhes bya la sogs so/
dus der snga phyir byon pa'i lo tsā ba/
/chen po lha yi bla ma ye shes 'od/
/rin chen bzang po grags 'byor shes rab dang/
/("bro) seng lar shākya 'od dang lhe zhi ba 'od/
/(rngog) legs pa'i shes rab (rgya) brtson 'grus seng ge dang/
/tshul khrims rgyal ba khu yi dngos grub 'bar/
/('brom) royal ba'i 'byung gnas shākya blo gros mtshan/
/(mar thung) chos kyi shes rab dad pa shes rab dang/
/(rma) dge ba' 1 blo gros ga rod tshul khrims 'byung (1. 3r) gnas
mtshan/
/(khyung po) chos kyi brtson 'grus stag lo gzhon brtson pa/
/'gar pa chos bzang she'u rdo rje lha/
/rab zhi bshes gnyen (rngog) blo Idan shes rab can/
/(pu hrang) legs pa'i shes rab 'phags pa shes rab dang/
/shakya ye shes ("brog mi) dga' ba'i rdo rje gzung/
/gyi lcang d bu dkar chos kyi yon tan dang/
/chos kyi rin chen (mar pa) chos kyi blo gros mtshan/
/gnyan lo dar ma grags dang 'gos Thas btsas/
leyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer (klog skya) shes rab brtsegs/
/(mal gyo) blo gros grags dang (se tsa) bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa/
/ rong pachos bzang (yol lcags) rdo rje dbang phyug dang/
/(mar 'od) byang chub shes rab tsa mi sangs rgyas grags/
/khe'u gad 'khor lo grags dang (spang zho) goal bar grags/
/ding ri chos grags sgyus kyi smon lam grags/
7pa tshab nyi grags ba ri rin chen grags/
/shes rab grags dang rwa chen rdo rje grags/
/kre bo sher dpal bkra shis rgyal mtshan pa/

/ba reg thog dga' rma ban chos 'bar dang/
Amtshur ston dbyig gi rgyal mtshan mthur dbang nge/
/(apyal) kun dga' rdo rje dang ni (dpyal) kun dga' grags/
mar do chos dbang chos kyi enying po dang/
/(kam) chos kyi ye shes (phyugs mtshams) lung rig rgya mtsho
dang/
/tshul. khrims yon tan khe'u gad yon dpal/
/bsod nams bzang po sum pa dpal mchog gi/
/rdo rje (f. 3v) dang ni nyi ma rdo rje dang/
/(khu) dge bonyen ne tso kog skya gzhon nu 'bar/
ha ston ye shes rgyal mtshan byang chub byung/
/(glan) chos kyi blo gros (cog gru) ting nge 'dzin bzang po/
/shes rab ye shes rig pa gzhon nu dang/ omission
/tshul khrims brtsegs pa dang ni lha btsun pa/
Lha btsal gu ni rā dza (mgog) sangs rgyas bskyangs/
/rgyal gyi lo tsa rdo rje (smal) rgyal po dang/
de ba rin chen (lha) chos kyi rin chen dang/
(sayur) tshul khrims 'od zer dge slong bya yi gdong/
/da byin lo tsa dang ni phur bu 'od/
pa tshab) tahul rgyal shes rab legs dang (nag tsho) dharma
grags/
mar pa blo gros bzang po se lo tsā/
/zla grage pa gnyal mi ye shes chos/
chos kyi bla ma dge slong shes rab bskyangs/
/nag tsho sher rgyan 'a zhwa rgya gar brtsegs/
/ gnyan ston bsod nams ba ri chos grags dang/
long po lo tsä gzhon nu shes rab dang/
/'gar pe sher 'byung 'jam đpal gzhon nu dang/
/shes rab 'od zer dang ni (lce) dga' ba a pal/
/ye shes byung gnas shākya brtson 'grus pa/
/rwa pa chos rab (lo btsun chung) rdo rje rgyal mtshan dang/
/zhwa ma dge benyen seng rgyal lce bkra shis/
/chag lo dgra bcom dpyal pa chos kyi bzang/
/(gnubs) byams pa'i dpal dang sa skya pandi ta/
/(chag) chos rje dpal dang shes rab od (apyal) dang zhang/
7 grub pa dpal dang (f. 4r) (glo bo) shes rab rin po che/
/(1ho brag) Tu ru dar ma seng ge mi mnyam bzang/
/shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan (shong) blo gros brtan/
/au di yā na rin chen dpal dang khams/
/blo gros rgyal po ldan ma tshul seng dang/
/ra sa gzhon brtson shu ke grags reyal mtshan/

it intended that the rab-byung should apply to the previous
lamas, rather than the successive?)

Bka'-brgyud-
ра
/BKA' BRGYUD PA'i grub mtha' byung tshul la/ so so'i
byung tshul/ ita sgom gyi mnam gzhag/ cung zad dpyad pa'o/
/dang po la/ bka' (. 9v) babs kyi gdams pa'i brgyud
'dzin pas na de skad bya/ dbye na mar pa'i brgyud 'dzin dang/
khyung po'i brgyud 'dzin gnyis/ tai lo pa la bka' babs bzhi'i
gdams pa mga' ba dang/ khyung po la ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro
ma gnyis kyi bka' babs mga' bas na de skad 10/
/phyag chen la mdo sngags gnyis/
dang po ni/ lhan cig skyes sbyor te/ zhen log mos gus
gtso bor ston cing/ dngos gzhi zhi lhag ngo sprod de/ rjes
snang thog tu rtsal sbyong ba dang/ sngags su gnyug sems kyi
ngo bo gtan la phab nas mnyam par bzhag pas rlung dbu mar augs

*/DPAL BRUG PA'I SGRUB THABS SKOR LNGA zhes pa bde mchog 'BRUG-PA

BKA'-BRGYUD-
PA PRECEPTS
byin rlabs kvi. skor zhes pa zhal gyis ma mai tri nas mar pa
dang/ ti phu pa nas ras chung la brgyud pa/ &tum po nus mthu'i

*/DPAL BRUG PA'I NYAMS LEN PHRAL DGOS KYI SKOR rdo rje
sems dpa'i nyes ltung 'khrud pa'i cho ga rgyal po dzah las
brgyud pa mar pa'i 'gyur/ kam ka ni'i cho ga ngen song. Egyun
gcod pa chos rgyal dzah las brgyud pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i rtsa
rgyud 'bum pa dang/ bshad rgyud 'od zer drwa ba la brten pa'i

VISIONARY
POEM OF MDO
MKHYEN-BRISE
ON RIS-MED
/gang zag dbang po rab 'bring ste/
/aud 'gro nyag phran mkha' lding gis/
/mthong bul (=2yul) ji bzhin 'bras bur rags/
/rang bzhin rdzoge pa chen po ni/
/rig pa car phog ngo 'phrod nas/
/gzung 'dzin mdud pa zhig pa'i tshe/
/sku dang thig le ngo sprod kyis/
/rig dang (or: rang) longs skur rtsal chen rdzogs/
/snang bzhi'i 'od goal mthar phyin tshe/
/chos can chos nyia klong du zad/
/gzhon nu bum sku'i dbyings su grol/
/stong gsal 'dus ma byas pa la/
/dge dang sdig pa'i mtshan ma bral/
/mayam nyid rig pa'i rgyal po la/
/sangs rgyas bzang pos phan ma btags/
/sems can ngan pas gnod ma bskyal/
/chos dbyings brdal khyab chen po la/
/sa dang lam gyi rtsis grangs zhig/
/myam nyid chen por ye sangs rgyas/
/phung khams ye nas lha'i rang bzhin/
/bsnyen cing sgrub pa thang re chad/
/snod bcud dag pa rab 'byams la/
/zhing khams bya ba logs su med/
/rdzogs phyag dbu na chen po yang
/rab 'bring tha ma'i blor 'tshams par/
chos longs sprul pa sku yi bka'/
/dgongs pa rten dang tshig tu shar/
/gdul bya'i dbang po'i skal ba ru/
7go lung ma nges sna tshogs pas/
/chos bgo brgyad khri bzhi stong byung/ (f. 117v)
/don la ma rig nyon monge dang/
/gzung 'dzin grol ba kho nar dgongs/
/rgyu dang 'bras bu'i lam nyid kyang/
/drangs nges ldem dgongs dus gzhal sogs/
/mtha' drug tshul bzhis sems can gyi/
log ita bsal zhing dad mos dang/
/yang dag lam du 'khrid phyir dgongs/
Inga phrag tha ma'i dus 'di ru/
/nyon mongs rags shing sdug bsngal 'phel/
/thabs mkhas spyod pa sna tshogs kyis/



VISIONARY
/khams abang mthun par ma byas na/
POEM OF MDO
MKHYEN-
/mtha' goig dag gis mi 'dul zhing/
BRTSE ON
/blo chung dag gis rjes mi slebs/
RIS-MED
don 'di rtogs par mdzod cig ang/ /zhes dang/ lung bstan
mang du gnang mthar sku las spros pa'i 'od zer gyis rtogs sgrib
phra ba ma lus pa sbyangs te bde ba chen po'i ye shes kyi byin
rlabs kyis rgyud yongs su smin par mdzad do/
STAG-SHAM
*/rig 'azin stag sham rdo rie'i gter lung las/
QUOTED
yon tan gdul bya smad kyi phyogs nas "byung:
rdo rje'i ming can brtul zhugs stobs pa che:
phyag rdzogs klong gyur rta mgrin bka' babs dang:
rdo rje gro lod zhal mjal ba'i:
skal ldan skyes bu de yis gdul bya sdud:
rdzu 'phrul sprul pa'i skal ldan mang 'byung nas:
kaņ thog phyogs su ston pa'i dpang du 'dug:
bshad sgrub bstan pa (f. 118r) gzhal du med pa 'byung:
zhes sogs rdo rje'i lung bstan du mas dpang po byas pa bzhin

Tshe-dbang-
nor-bu
ra'i zhal yang yang mjal/ sku tshe snga ma'i yongs 'dzin mang
po'i mtshan gsal bar ston/ dbang skur chos 'chad/ ting 'dzin
sgom pa/ zab gter 'don cing gnas ago 'byed pa sogs phal pa'i
spyod yul las 'das pa'i gzhon nu rol rtsed tsam gyis kyang
dpyod ldan rams yid rang dbang med par 'phrog/ gzhan sems
mkhyen pa'i mungon shes dang/ bde gsal mi rtog pa'i nyams myong
rtsol med du shar ba soge sgo du ma nas dam pa'i skyes bu'i
sprul par yongs su grags kyang/ skal pa dman pa 'ga' zhig gi
log rtog bsal ba'i phyir gong ma'i dpon rigs su gtogs pa bla
ma kun bzang zhes pa zhig gis rig 'dzin stag sham rdo rje dang/
gter chen rol pa'i rdo rje zung la lung bstan zhus pa 'khrul
med kyi gzengs bstod gnang bas the tshom gyi min pa dbyings
su sangs/ gang ltar yang (f. 120r) dgung lo lnga par ljags
klog phul bas tshegs med du mkhyen/ drug par gter chen bla ma
las zab gsang rdzogs pa chen po'i smin grol gean pa nas bzung
phal cher 'bral med du bzhuge/ dgung lo bdun par rdo rje gro
lod kyi las byang blor bzung zhing yi dam mdzad pas bskyed rim
gsal brtan gyad du syur/ brgyad par sangs gling gter byon
thuge rje chen po'i rayab chos yang gsang 'od dra la gzigs pas
go ba dpyis phyin par 'khrungs shing/ gsang sngags spyi'i lta
spyod la nges pa rnyed/
bcu par ndo sngags la mkhyen pa rgyas pas dpyod ldan gyi
khengs pa'i spobs pa zil gyis man/ bou gcig par gter chen
bla ma las rang gter mkha' 'gro snying tig gi smin grol zab
rgyas su gsan pas gnas lugs la 'phrig tshud/ mal lam nam 'dod
du zin/ dregs pa can gyis srog snying phul/ bcu gnyis par rig
'azin 'gyur med rdo rje'i thugs sras orgyan mam grol las snga
'gyur mdo sgyu sems gsum gyi smin grol sogs rgya cher gsan/
khyad par dgung grangs bcu gsum bźes skabs gter chen bla ma
las amar tshang lugs kyi phyag chen dang/ rang gter rdzogs pa
chen po'i nyams khrid gnad smin du gsan pas rtogs pa'i bogs
thon/ lo de'i mjug tu 'jang chu ri bkra dgon du spyan drengs
nas grub chen (f. 120v) mchog gi sprul pa'i skur mnga' gsol/
rje dbon bla ma skal bzang orgyan bstan'azin nas brtse bas
bskyangs/ bcu bzhi par kaly thog rgyal sras bsod nams lde btsan
phyogs der phebs/ rje dbon bla ma skal bzang las bdud 'dul gter
chos bzhugs so 'tshal dang/ rtse le'i bka' 'bum sogs gsan/
tshur klong goal rtsa gsum skor gyi dbang lung yongs rdzogs
gnang ba sogs legs par gaan cing/ rgyal sras mchog nas phyi
mtha' gzigs pa'i thugs la shin tu btags/ bar khrod lha khang
du rig 'dzin padma chos rgyal spyan drangs shing bum sgrub
btsugs pe'i skabs/ bla ma skal bzang nas rje de nyid kyi gter

GTER-STON
Tshe-dbang-
nor-bu
nyer brgyad par slar brag 1 jongs nas rgyangs phu gangs
rar phebs/ sgrub pa la bzhugs/ dregs pa can gyi cho 'phrul
brtul zhugs kyis spa bkong/ lo de'i dbyar thog rtag brtan de'u
sogs kyi lha khang rten dang brten par bcas pa gsar du bzhengs/
chos kyi char phab/ ston brag la brgyud byang kong zhes nyang
po gzhung nas 'ol ka sogs la lam mdzad/ khra 'brug bsam yas
lha sa sogs la phyag mchod gnang nas mtshur phur phebs/ karma,
pa byang chub rdo rje dang/ chwa dmar chos kyi don grub lhan
rgyas su mjal/ zhwa dmar rin po cher dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa

dang/ zhang zhung gi yul mthar mon gyi ling pa/ ma ha tsi nar

60 "dor ba la zhum pa med pa'i lhag bsam khyad par can gyis/ mdo

yang bral zhing/ phyag len phra rags thams cad rang rang gi

pa cher mi ndzad/
writings
brtsams pa'i abang du byas na/ thos bsam gyi rim pa nthar
son cing lhag pa'i lhas rjes su bzung ba sogs rtsom pa'i rgyu
gsum thams cad tshang ma bstan bcos ji lta bu zhig rtsom kyang
thogs pa mi mnga' mod/ bla ma gong ma rdo rje 'chang dang zhal
mi gnyis pa de mams kyi legs par bshad pa'i rgyun la gnod dogs
gsung rtsom rgya cher ma mdzad kyang/ zhu ba po so so'i blo dang
mthun par bka' rtsom phran bu gnang ba la/ dus 'khor/ bla ma
zhi khro'i tshe dbang/ geo (f. 173r) rig rgyud bzhi mnams kyi
brgyud 'debs/ gsung ngag rin po che/ 'jigs byed dbang brgyud lugs
gsum/smar khrid tshem bu lugs/ nā ro mkha' spyod/ gar zhal mnams
kyi brgyud 'debs kyi kha skong/ sgrol ma'i gsol 'debs/ rmor chen
mchog sprul myur phebs/ yab rje bsod nams rin chen/ beo brgyad

'jug sogs gsan/ gzhan yang bla ma mang po las mdo sngags kyi

la brtsams nas/ yang shar brgyud/ gser pa'i sa'i thig ler/

btab/ mthar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang (f. 206v) bcas gdan
sa de nyid du gshegs so/

SA-SKYA-PA
BIOGRAPHY
Bkra-shis-
bzang-po
kyis/ sku tshe ang 'dir yang gzhan phan gyi thugs bskyed
la gcig tu gzhol zhing bzod pa thob pa dang/ rig 'dzin sngags
kyi sdom pa rnams kyang tshul bzhin du legs par nos te/ thos
pa dang bsam pa dang sgom pa phul du phyin cing/ rgyud sde
rgya mtshor 'jug pa'1 ded dpon chen por dbang bagyur nas/ ming
tsam dang brda tsam dang tha snyad tsam ma yin par rgyud sde
mtha' dag gi dbang dang byin rlabs kyi rim pa rjes gnang khrid
lung zhal shes kyi gdams pa rab tu gnas pa dang/ rdo rje slob
dpon gyis bgyi bar 'os pa'i phyag len gyi rim pa che para chung
gsum mtha' dag sogs kyis bstan pa rin po che spyi dang/ khyad
par chos grwa chen po lhun grub steng gi rgyan dam par sku drin
yun du che ba zhig ni yin par/ nges par don gyis rdo rje 'chang
dbang dam par go zhing/ bdag cag nas kyang sbas pa'i mal 'byor
de nyid kyi zhal las bcom ldan 'das 'khor lo sdom pa dpal mkha'
'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil khor (1. 207r) du dbang bskur ba to
metaa ngor chen rdo rje chang gi gsung rab dri ma med pa'i
steng nas legs par nos pas/ rang nyid dang yang tshe rabs thog
ma med pa nas smon lam gyi las skal shin tu bzang ba zhig
mchis/zhes dang/ bla rgan nyid kyang dgung lo grangs mang ba
bcas zhabs "ban gyis benyun run ring bas/ nged nas kun rig
dbang dang rjes gnang goig gyis tsam phul/ zla ba bdun pa'i
nang gi tshes bou skor tsam nas bsnyung gzhi nyob shas 'dra
mo zhig gis baun cu don bdun pa tshes nyi shu la dag pa'1 zhing
du pabegshegs/ zhag gsum gyi bar 'od gsal chen po'i ngang
du gnas/ thugs dam gsal 'debs dang sku gdung chas zhugs kyi
zhabs phyi rams ci ltar dgos pa nged rang nas bsgrubs/ gdung
gi me mchod bshes gyen dam pa bla ma nam mkha' apal bzang gis
phul bar mdzad/sku gdung chas chugs dang sbyin sreg gi skabs
nam mkha' thams cad 'ja' od kyis khengs pa dang/ lhag par nub
phyoga kyi nam mkha'i phyogs thams cad 'ja' sprin rma bya'1
ngrin pa lta bus khyab pa soge byung/ gdung rus rams bying la
sātstsha btab chu bo chen mor gdan drangs/ nyung shas la sku
brnyan dang sätstsha btab pa bcas la byang chub mchod rten mda'
tshad ma zhig bzhengs te 'jam mgon sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyi
sku gdung bzhugs pa'i lha khang du bzhugs (f. 207v) su gsol/
aku chas mams ji ltar yod pa sa skyong khri chen bla ma dang/
nged nas zhabs 'gyur zhus pas bsod nams kyi skal ba shin tu
che bar mchis/ /zhes so
*/yang rtogs briod de nyid las/ lo dar gyis stod smad gang
du'ang bum gter sum brgya nas brgya phrag lhag pa'i bar begrubs
te so sor phan cha byed par/ sgrub tshul kyang mang du mchis
rung/ phral phug thams cad du dge phyir sangs rgyas klu dbang

RJE "DZIN PA BKRA SHIS BZANG PO'i mam thar thor bur gsungs pa
ni/ dan pa de nyia nỉ ghi tshul khrim8 nam par dag pa la Emas
pa dang/ theg chen rgyal ba'i sras po'i 'jug sgo rin po che de
nyid tshe rabs du mar sbyangs pa mthar phyin pa'i stobs kyis/
sku tshe'dir yang guhan phan eyi thugs bskyed la gcig tu gzol
zhing bzod pa thob padang/ rig 'azin sngags kyi sdom pa rams
kyang tshul bzhin du legs par nos te/ thos pa dang bsam pa darl
sgom pa phul du phyin cing/ rgyud sae reya mtshor'jug pa'i.
ded dpon chen por abang bagyur nas/ ming tsam dang brda tsam
dang tha snyad tsam ma yin par rgyud sde mtha' dag gi dbang
dang byin rlabs kyi rim pa rjes gnang khrid lung zhal shes
kyi gdams pa rab tu gnas pa dang/ rdo rje slob doon gyis beyi
bar 'os pa'i phyag len gyi rim pa che phra chung gsum mtha'
dag sogs kyis bstan pa rin po che spyi dang/ khyad par chos
grwa chen po lhun grub steng gi reyan dam par sku drin yun du
che ba zhig ni yin par/ nges par don gyis rdo rje 'chang dbang
dam par go zhing/ bdag cag nas kyang sbas pa'i rmal 'byor de
nyid kyi zhal las bcom ldan 'das khor lo sdom pa dpal micha!
"gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil (f. 207r) 'khor du abang bskur ba ngor

nas smon lam eyi las skal shin tu bzang ba zhig mchis/ zhes
dang/ bla rgan nyid kyang dgung lo grangs mang ba bcas zhabs
"bam gyis banyun yun ring bas/ aged nas kun rig dbang dang rjes

don bdun pa tshes nyi shu la dag pa'i zhing du gahegs/ zhag

"debs dang sku gdung chas zhugs kyi zhabs phyi rnams ci ltar
dgos pa nged rang nas bsgrubs/ gdung gi me mchod bshes anyen
dam pa bla ma nam mkha' dpal bzang gis phul bar mdzad/ sku
gdung chas zhugs dang sbyin sree gi skabs sam mkha thams cad
'ja' 'od kyis khenge pa dang/ lhag par nub phyogs kyi nam mkha'i
phyogs thams cad 'ja' sprin rma bya'i mgrin pa ita bus khyab pa
sogs byung/ gdung rus rams bying la sätstsha btab chu bo chen
mor gdan drangs/ nyung shas la sku brnyandang sätstsha btab pa

"jam mgon sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyi sku gdung bzhugs pa'i

so/
/yang rtogs brjod de nyid las/ lo dar gyis stod smad gang

rung/ 'phral phug thams cad du dge phyir sangs rgyas klu dbang'

nams spel phyir/ de'i meron du nor iha pho mo/ lha klu gzhi
bdag gia bekor ba dang/ sa bdag klu gnyan dang sde brgyad kyi
nad las grol ba'i phyir/ klu abang rgyal po'i lha tshogs la
seng ge sgra dang iha klu mnams kyis bskor ba zhig dang/ de dag

editor of phyag rdzas kho na'i steng nas'jam mgon bla ma'i gsung rab
the unpub- engar spar du ma 'khod pa yongs su rdzogs par blod/
lished works gan sa chen pod pal spungs su gser eyi rgya phtbs che legs

sum khri bdun stong Inga brgya so goig byung bar bshad la/
ston pa zhal bzhugs pa'i dus rgyal po'i (f. 22v) khab tu
gzugs can snying po dang/ de'i sras ma skyes dgra sogs bstan
pa la gus pas mchod pa mang po dang/ bar skabs su chos rgyal
chen po mya ngan med dang/ phyis su rgyal po dharma pā la
sogs kyi bde bar gshegs pa'i ring lugs mtha' dag la bsnyen
bkur rgya cher mdzad do/
/bod yul dbus su rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul gyi rgyal rigs
las son pa chos rgyal gnya' khri btsun (sic!) po sogs gnam
gyi khri bdun/ bar eyi steng gnyis dang legs drug (15)/ sa yi
ede brgyad/ log gi btsan bzhi ste nyer bdun rim par byon pa'i
dus su chab srid sgrungs dang dhe'u bon rams kyis bskyangs/
tho ri gnyan btsan (28) gyi dus su za ma tog sogs nam
mkha' nas babs te dam pa'i chos kyi abu brnyes/
de nas rgyal rabs inga pa rgyal po srong btsan sgam po
(33) dang/ de nas gdung rabs bzhi pa khri sde gtsug brtan (37)/
de'i sras khri srong lde'u btsan/ de'i sras mu ni btsan po
(39) dang/ sad na legs 'jings yon (mu tig btsan po)/
de'i sras minga' bdag khri ral pa can sogs kyis sangs
rgyas kyi bstan pa nyin mo ltar mdzad/ de nas re zhig glang
dar mas bsten pa banub kyang/ de'i sras 'od srungs dang yum
brtan gnyis las stod la mga' ris pa yul abus sogs su gdung
brgyud byung ba mnams kyis kyang/ rang rang gi stobs 'byor
dang bstun pa' 1 (f. 23r) bstan pa la sri zhu rgya cher mdzad

ma byung zhing/ de tsam nas rje btsun sa skya pa chen po

khri skor bcu gsum gyi bdag por mga' gsol ba nas lo brgyad
cu tsam bskyangs/

nas/ dbus phyogs phal cher ni tā si byang chub rgyal mtshan

yang bzung nas/ lo brgyad cu gya bdun gyi bar du dbus gtsang
gi mthil rams sde srid phag mo gru pas abang mdzad/

kyi rigs las byung pa ste/ de yang bod khams 'dir mi'i 'gro

(Grub chen sangs rgyas ngon po nas brgyud pa'i bo dong lugs)
ff. 92
-- gdong; (v) Mkhyen brtse'i bka' 'bun
Author: Mkhyen brtse'i-dbang-po
Edition: Rdzong-gear
TOOLS
/na mo guru dā ki sip ha mu khi yi sarba shatrū na bi ghnām
nã ra va phat/
Abyad ma'bum rdug gi 'khor lo chen mo/ theg pa chen po las
thams cad grub pa zhes bya ba'i mdo) ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma
seng ge'i gdong pa car ma'i lha tshoge rnans la phyes 'tshal 1o/
gang phyir ruan rtog 8.yo med legs grub rgya ntsho'i dpal
"bar ma gdod nas rang byung ye shes rayas pa'i dpal gyi 'od/

dril ba (ff. 42v-46r)

brgyad kyis bsdus pa ste zag pa dang bcas pa'o/

bcas pa thams cad las yang dag par "das pa zag med kyi bde
ba chen po rgyun chad (f. 42v) med pa'o/

bu ste/ spang bar bya ba ma yin pas don dam gzhan stong/

bsdus pa sdug bsngal dang skad cig las ma 'das te/ las dang
nyon mongs kyis sbrul sdug bsngal gyi rang bzhin no

gang gis kyang ma bskyed cing sdug bsngal med pa'i bde ba
chen po rgyun chad med pa'o/

pa'o/

gi don dang gzhan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa'i gnas so/
